let loadedCallback = () => {
  if(window.location.pathname != '/loss-and-damage'){
  document.getElementsByClassName("header-display-desktop")[0]
    .insertAdjacentHTML("beforebegin", '<div class="climate-clock-wrapper"><climate-clock /></div>');}

  // Make nav "buttons" work like links on desktop
  let navFolderLinks = [
    "/science",
    "/about"
  ]
  document.querySelectorAll('.header-display-desktop .header-nav-folder-title')
    .forEach((el, idx) => {
      if (idx != 0) return // kludge!
      el.href = navFolderLinks[idx]
      el.addEventListener("click", ev => {
        ev.preventDefault()
        window.open(navFolderLinks[idx], "_self")  
      })
    })
};

if (document.readyState === "complete" || (document.readyState !== "loading" && !document.documentElement.doScroll)) {
  loadedCallback();
} else {
  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", loadedCallback);
}

      <div class="sqs-layout sqs-grid-12 columns-12" data-type="page-section" id="page-section-60ca88d8f262a40f42f74472"><div class="row sqs-row"><div class="col sqs-col-12 span-12"><div class="row sqs-row"><div class="col sqs-col-9 span-9"><div class="sqs-block code-block sqs-block-code" data-block-type="23" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1624042006288_6967"><div class="sqs-block-content"><a name="action"></a></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-ad7ac267acd497a00a75"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<h1 style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><br>2. an <a href="https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLScMZewLRZC3pk3kdZbTsB6DalpV6nCoPXUWVRR02CKERLEmWg/viewform" target="">Action clock</a> in your hands.</h1>


</div></div></div><div class="col sqs-col-3 span-3"><div class="sqs-block spacer-block sqs-block-spacer" data-aspect-ratio="7.222222222222222" data-block-type="21" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1623894554424_8413"><div class="sqs-block-content sqs-intrinsic" style="padding-bottom: 7.22222%;" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1665748086465_97">&nbsp;</div></div></div></div><div class="sqs-block spacer-block sqs-block-spacer" data-aspect-ratio="32.082324455205814" data-block-type="21" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1623896215401_10229"><div class="sqs-block-content sqs-intrinsic" style="padding-bottom: 32.0823%;" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1665748086465_100">&nbsp;</div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1623889367538_7490"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<p class="sqsrte-large" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Perfect for schools, universities and offices, <strong>this clock is portable and built for action. </strong></p><p class="sqsrte-large" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Want one in your classroom? Want to put a clock on the desk of your favorite climate-champion? Know a climate <em>denier</em> who needs to get "clocked"? </p><p class="sqsrte-large" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><em>Until we expand production, we have </em><strong><em>a limited supply of action clocks</em></strong><em> for sale at a sliding scale. Get on the waitlist (or tell us why you urgently need a clock) by filling our </em><a href="https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLScMZewLRZC3pk3kdZbTsB6DalpV6nCoPXUWVRR02CKERLEmWg/viewform" target=""><em>this form</em></a>.</p><p class="sqsrte-large" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Or you can <a href="https://climateclock.world/make" target="_blank">build your own</a> with our DIY Maker Instructions! (Questions?Ask our maker team in the tech-team channel of the slack workspace. <a href="https://join.slack.com/t/climate-clock/shared_invite/zt-dgy8tdxj-ziLh0WV7dwlYrinSUXmnNg" target="">Join here</a>.)</p>


</div></div></div></div></div>
    </div>
  </div>
  
</section>

      <div class="sqs-layout sqs-grid-12 columns-12" data-type="page-section" id="page-section-60ca891f320a281d2ff721ff"><div class="row sqs-row"><div class="col sqs-col-12 span-12"><div class="sqs-block code-block sqs-block-code" data-block-type="23" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1624042006288_12362"><div class="sqs-block-content"><a name="digital"></a></div></div></div></div><div class="row sqs-row"><div class="col sqs-col-12 span-12"><div class="row sqs-row"><div class="col sqs-col-12 span-12"><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-4045ded5eda8202469d0"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<h1 style="white-space:pre-wrap;">3. a <a href="https://github.com/beautifultrouble/climate-clock-widget" target="_blank">DIGITAL Clock</a> on your Website.</h1>


</div></div></div><div class="col sqs-col-0 span-0"></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1623891758928_10497"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<h3 style="white-space:pre-wrap;">REMIND EVERY VISITOR THAT WE MUST #ACTINTIME.</h3><p class="sqsrte-large" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">To add the Climate Clock widget to your site, <strong>all you have to do is add the following HTML:</strong></p>


</div></div><div class="row sqs-row"><div class="col sqs-col-1 span-1"><div class="sqs-block spacer-block sqs-block-spacer sized vsize-1" data-block-type="21" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1623892032555_81715"><div class="sqs-block-content">&nbsp;</div></div></div><div class="col sqs-col-11 span-11"><div class="sqs-block code-block sqs-block-code" data-block-type="23" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1623892032555_7466"><div class="sqs-block-content"><pre class="source-code"><div><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&lt;</span><span class="cm-tag">script</span> <span class="cm-attribute">src</span>=<span class="cm-string">"https://climateclock.world/widget-v2.js"</span> <span class="cm-attribute">async</span><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&gt;</span><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&lt;/</span><span class="cm-tag">script</span><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&gt;</span>
<span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&lt;</span><span class="cm-tag">climate-clock</span> <span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">/&gt;</span></div></pre></div></div></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1623892032555_61645"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<h4 style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><br>TROUBLESHOOTING:</h4><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><em>Some websites won’t recognize the </em><strong>&lt;climate-clock&gt;</strong><em> tag. If your website filters HTML in this way, ask a website tech how to add it directly.<br></em></p></li><li><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><em>If the Climate Clock widget displays incorrectly on your site, you can try an </em><strong><em>older version</em></strong><em> with a different appearance:</em></p></li></ul>


</div></div><div class="row sqs-row"><div class="col sqs-col-1 span-1"><div class="sqs-block spacer-block sqs-block-spacer sized vsize-1" data-block-type="21" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1623892032555_76312"><div class="sqs-block-content">&nbsp;</div></div></div><div class="col sqs-col-11 span-11"><div class="sqs-block code-block sqs-block-code" data-block-type="23" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1623892032555_14074"><div class="sqs-block-content"><pre class="source-code"><div><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&lt;</span><span class="cm-tag">script</span> <span class="cm-attribute">src</span>=<span class="cm-string">"https://climateclock.world/widget-v1.js"</span> <span class="cm-attribute">async</span><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&gt;</span><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&lt;/</span><span class="cm-tag">script</span><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&gt;</span>
<span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&lt;</span><span class="cm-tag">climate-clock</span> <span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">/&gt;</span></div></pre></div></div></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1623892032555_69632"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<h4 style="white-space:pre-wrap;">For Advanced Users:</h4><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">If you prefer, <a href="https://github.com/BeautifulTrouble/climate-clock-widget" target="_blank">clone the Climate Clock widget</a>, build it from source and host it on your own server. Want to make changes? Open an issue or contribute a pull request on github!</p>


</div></div></div></div></div>
    </div>
  </div>

<h2 style="text-align:center;white-space:pre-wrap;">(Here’s the big secret.)</h2>


</div></div><div class="row sqs-row"><div class="col sqs-col-2 span-2"><div class="sqs-block spacer-block sqs-block-spacer" data-aspect-ratio="102.27272727272727" data-block-type="21" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1623895837891_7917"><div class="sqs-block-content sqs-intrinsic" style="padding-bottom: 102.273%;" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1665748086465_106">&nbsp;</div></div></div><div class="col sqs-col-8 span-8"><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1623895837891_10519"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<p style="text-align:center;white-space:pre-wrap;" class="">The Clocks are powerful tools. But the <em>real</em> power of this project is in how we use them together. <a href="/join">Join&nbsp;the climate clock network</a>, and tell us about you and your team.</p>


</div></div></div><div class="col sqs-col-2 span-2"><div class="sqs-block spacer-block sqs-block-spacer sized vsize-1" data-block-type="21" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1623895837891_10455"><div class="sqs-block-content">&nbsp;</div></div></div></div></div></div></div>
